./.github/copilot-instructions.md:133:The renderer can only call the channels declared in `electron/preload.ts` via `window.veniceForge`. In **Electron mode**, the renderer cannot choose arbitrary Venice endpoints or read the raw API key (it lives in `safeStorage` in the main process).
./.github/copilot-instructions.md:202:Any code that differs between Electron and web **must** use `isElectron()` from `src/services/desktopBridge.ts`. ./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:143:  - P2: Legacy direct window.veniceForge.chat.* in chat-store.ts explicitly documented with AGENTS reference (no new calls added).
./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:290:- **venice() dropped AbortSignal (BUG-1 / P1):** `venice()` in `src/lib/venice-client.ts` did not forward `options.signal` to `desktopVenice.request()`. When the renderer aborted a stream, `parseSSEStream` cancelled the local reader but the upstream HTTPS request in the main process kept running and consumed tokens. Fix: pass `options.signal` as the second positional arg of `desktopVenice.request()`, which is the documented `AbortSignal` parameter. `desktopVenice.request()` calls `attachAbort(signalId, signal)` which registers an abort listener that invokes `window.veniceForge.venice.abort(signalId)` on cancel.
./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:400:- **Lint gate:** `src/stores/chat-store.ts` no longer trips `--max-warnings=0`; the `as any` cast on the legacy `window.veniceForge.chat.save` call is replaced with a typed `as unknown as StoredConversation` cast against the IPC contract.
./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:623:- Electron main process with strict IPC validation (`validateVeniceIpcRequest`), sandboxed renderer, context isolation, and preload bridge (`window.veniceForge`).

./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:5:Format follows [Keep a Changelog](https://keepachangelog.com/en/1.1.0/). Venice Forge uses [Semantic Versioning](https://semver.org/spec/v2.0.0.html).
./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:127:- **Character image rendering on the webserver `/characters` view:** When the Venice `/characters` response omits every recognized image field (`photoUrl` / `photo_url` / `avatarUrl` / `avatar_url` / `imageUrl` / `image_url` / `profileImageUrl` / `profile_image_url` / `image` / `avatar` / `profileImage` / `profile_image`, plus the nested `url` / `src` / `href` for object values), the `Avatar` component in `src/components/CharactersView.tsx` was falling back to initials like `SA, VE, BA, IS, AI, CA`. `src/utils/characterImageResolver.ts` now constructs the canonical photo URL `https://outerface.venice.ai/api/characters/{id}/photo` from a safe `id` (or `slug` as fallback) — the host is already in the 3-host `VENICE_CHARACTER_IMAGE_HOSTS` allowlist, and the id is double-validated against `SAFE_CHARACTER_ID_RE = /^[A-Za-z0-9][A-Za-z0-9_.-]{0,127}$/`, so SSRF controls stay strict. Added `isSafeCharacterId()` and `buildSyntheticCharacterPhotoUrl()` exports; the `RESOLVER` test file gained 12 new cases (synthetic fallback, isSafeCharacterId, buildSyntheticCharacterPhotoUrl) with `REGRESSION GUARD` comments.
./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:213:- **Local master YAML config system:** Optional YAML files (`config.yaml`, `themes.yaml`) let developers and power users configure Venice Forge without touching the UI. Locations follow a strict precedence: env override (`VENICE_FORGE_CONFIG_FILE`) > repo-local (dev) > userData (packaged) > built-in defaults. The schema (v1) covers app identity, secret import policy, theme selection, default model selections, chat parameters, memory options, research defaults, character defaults, and developer flags. Plaintext `secrets.venice_api_key` / `secrets.jina_api_key` in the YAML are imported into OS secure storage (`safeStorage`) on startup and then redacted from the file (unless `secrets.keep_plaintext_keys: true` is explicitly set). Default config files never contain real keys. Three CLI scripts are bundled: `npm run config:init` (copy example templates to `.config/*.local.yaml`), `npm run config:validate` (parse + validate without launching Electron), and `npm run config:print` (print the sanitized effective config; never raw keys). A new **Settings → Local Config** section shows the resolved paths, source, parse errors, validation warnings, key import status, and provides Reload / Open Folder / Export Template / Clear Secure Store actions. See [`docs/CONFIG.md`](../DEVELOPMENT/CONFIG.md) for the full schema and security model. The local-files-only rule is enforced (`looksLikeUrl()` rejects `http://`, `https://`, and any scheme-bearing path), control characters in paths are rejected, and the existing child-safety guard runs on every prompt path regardless of config source.

./AGENTS.md:158:**Model-aware recipe contract (Phase 2A).** `src/config/image-model-capabilities.ts` is the single source of truth for which image model supports which fields. The registry exports `getImageModelCapabilities`, `buildDimensionOptions`, `isDimensionSupported`, `normalizeDimensionsForModel`, `getUnsupportedRecipeFields`, and `getRecipeCapabilityList`. `src/types/project.ts` adds `getRecipeCompatibilityReport(recipe, caps, modelIsKnown)` which returns `{ status: 'compatible' | 'partial' | 'incompatible', issues, sanitizedRecipe, unsupportedFields }`. The Image Studio (`src/components/image/image-view.tsx`) reads the live capability contract and (a) hides controls the model does not support, (b) shows a small "Capabilities" line, and (c) passes per-field `supports*` flags into `buildImagePayload` so the network boundary drops `negative_prompt` / `style_preset` / `steps` / `cfg_scale` / `seed` when the model does not accept them. The Media Inspector (`src/components/gallery/media-inspector.tsx`) renders the `RecipeCompatibilityCard` (status + issues + use-with-current-model + use-original + show/hide comparison) and an "Export recipe" button alongside the existing "Copy recipe" action. The `verify:model-aware-recipes` audit script (`scripts/verify-model-aware-recipes.cjs`) is part of the `verify:workspace-contracts` parity. See `VERIFY-043`.
./AGENTS.md:170:**Prompt Library Foundation (Phase 2D).** `src/types/prompt-library.ts` defines the canonical `PromptKind` union (chat / system / image / negative / research / character / workflow / recipe / general), `PromptScope` (global / project), `PromptVersion` (append-only per-prompt version chain), `PromptLibraryItem` (id, currentVersionId, versions, scope, projectId, tags, favorite, archivedAt, modelHints, variables), and the JSON-serialisable `PromptLibraryExport` envelope. The `sanitizePromptLibraryItem` and `sanitizePromptVersion` helpers reject / redact `sk-…` / `venice_…` / `Bearer …` / `Authorization:` payloads and cap every field so a corrupt record cannot inflate the storage budget. `isPromptSecretLike` and `redactPromptSecrets` are the canonical secret-detection helpers used by the save / import / export paths. `src/stores/prompt-library-store.ts` is a thin Zustand store: `ensureLoaded` hydrates from the `promptLibrary` IndexedDB store (added by `dbMigrations` toVersion 8 and registered in `STORE_NAMES` / `ENCRYPTED_STORES`), `createPrompt` / `updatePrompt` / `addPromptVersion` / `setCurrentVersion` / `archivePrompt` / `unarchivePrompt` / `deletePrompt` / `toggleFavorite` mutate + persist atomically, and `importPrompts` / `exportPrompts` round-trip through the safe envelope. `src/components/prompts/PromptLibraryView.tsx` is mounted in `App.tsx` for the canonical `prompts` tab and lists / edits / versions / archives / deletes prompts with a confirm-gated delete flow. The Image Studio and Media Inspector expose "Save to Prompt Library" actions on the prompt / negative prompt / recipe fields; the Command Palette renders a Prompt Library section (Open / New / Use Selected / Export / Import) routed through the canonical tab registry. The `verify:prompt-library` audit script (`scripts/verify-prompt-library.cjs`) is wired into the `ci` parity command. See `VERIFY-046`.
./AGENTS.md:172:**Scene Composer Foundation (Phase 2E).** `src/types/scene.ts` defines the canonical `SceneComponentKind` union (subject / character / location / mood / style / camera / lighting / composition / negative / note), `SceneComponent` (kind, title, content, enabled), `SceneMediaRef`, `ScenePromptRef`, `SceneVersion` (append-only version chain with components + mediaRefs + promptRefs), `SceneComposerItem` (id, scope, projectId, currentVersionId, versions, defaultModel, defaultWidth, defaultHeight, defaultAspectRatio, outputMediaIds, tags, favorite, archivedAt), and the JSON-serialisable scene export envelope. The `sanitizeSceneComposerItem`, `sanitizeSceneVersion`, and `sanitizeSceneComponent` helpers reject / redact `sk-…` / `venice_…` / `Bearer …` / `Authorization:` payloads and cap every field. `isSecretLike` and `redactSecrets` are the canonical secret-detection helpers. `src/stores/scene-composer-store.ts` is a thin Zustand store: `ensureLoaded` hydrates from the `scenes` IndexedDB store (added by `dbMigrations` toVersion 9 and registered in `STORE_NAMES` / `ENCRYPTED_STORES`), `createScene` / `updateScene` / `addSceneVersion` / `setCurrentVersion` / `archiveScene` / `unarchiveScene` / `deleteScene` / `toggleFavorite` / `addOutputMedia` / `removeOutputMedia` mutate + persist atomically, and `importScenes` / `exportScenes` round-trip through the safe envelope. `src/services/sceneCompiler.ts` exports `compileSceneToRecipe` which combines components in canonical order (subject→character→location→mood→style→camera→lighting→composition→note), extracts negative/style, maps defaults, and outputs `GenerationRecipe`. `src/components/scenes/SceneComposerView.tsx` is mounted in `App.tsx` for the canonical `scenes` tab with a split layout (list + detail), component grid, version history, compile+send-to-image-studio, copy-recipe, and confirm-gated delete. The `verify:scene-composer` audit script (`scripts/verify-scene-composer.cjs`) is wired into the `ci` parity command. See `VERIFY-047`.

./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:134:- **Phase 2A model-aware recipes (VERIFY-043):** Expanded the image model capability registry with `isDimensionSupported`, `normalizeDimensionsForModel`, `getUnsupportedRecipeFields`, and `getRecipeCapabilityList` helpers. Image Studio now hides negative-prompt / seed / style / steps controls when the selected model does not support them, surfaces a live "Capabilities" line, and passes per-field `supports*` flags into `buildImagePayload` so the network boundary drops `negative_prompt` / `style_preset` / `steps` / `cfg_scale` / `seed` when unsupported. ./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:208:- **Media Studio (Library revamp):** The previous generated-image Library has been rebuilt as Media Studio — a single local-first hub for every image and video Venice Forge has generated. The new `MediaItem` shape (with `mediaType`, `operation`, `parentId`, `childrenIds`, `tags`, `note`, `favorite`, `sha256`, `exportedPathToken`) is added in-place to the existing encrypted `images` IndexedDB store via the idempotent `migrateGalleryImageToMediaItem` migrator; no destructive store migration. New modules: `src/types/media.ts`, `src/services/mediaMigration.ts`, `src/stores/media-store.ts` (transient Zustand cache, IDB is source of truth, exports `selectById` / `selectChildren` / `selectParent` / `filterMedia` / `sortMedia` / `searchMedia`), `src/utils/mediaItem.ts` (pure helpers: `mediaItemSource`, `mediaCapabilities`, formatting), `src/hooks/useMediaThumb.ts` (in-memory LRU canvas thumbnails for web), and `src/components/gallery/{media-card,media-toolbar,media-detail-dialog,media-inspector}.tsx`. The view is renamed "Media Studio" in the sidebar, header, TABS row, page copy, and empty state. Image tools (`image-tools.tsx`) and the video view (`video-view.tsx`) now auto-persist their results as MediaItems with the correct `operation` and `parentId` (verify-020 regression guard). The main-process side gains a strict-path-validation disk service (`electron/services/mediaService.ts`) and five new IPC channels: `app:media:export`, `app:media:import`, `app:media:reveal`, `app:media:meta`, `app:media:thumb`. Reveal and meta are allowed only for paths under `Pictures/Venice Forge`, `Desktop`, `Downloads`, `Documents`, `<userData>/metadata/media-thumbs`, and `<userData>/metadata/media-exports`; export writes to `Pictures/Venice Forge/Media Studio/<sub>/<file>` via atomic temp+rename; import is capped at 50 MiB; filenames are sanitized to `[a-zA-Z0-9_.-]` and subfolders to `[a-zA-Z0-9_-]` with length caps. The "Show in folder" button is disabled until an item has an `exportedPathToken` (set by `app:media:export`), with a tooltip explaining why. Per-model capabilities (upscale / edit / video / vision) are surfaced in the inspector. Web mode falls back to a browser anchor for export and an in-memory canvas thumbnail cache. 60 new tests across 6 files (`mediaMigration`, `media-store`, `mediaItem`, `gallery-view`, `image-tools`, `electron/services/mediaService`). See [`docs/MEDIA_STUDIO.md`](../design/MEDIA_STUDIO.md).
./docs/audits/CHANGELOG.md:213:- **Local master YAML config system:** Optional YAML files (`config.yaml`, `themes.yaml`) let developers and power users configure Venice Forge without touching the UI. Locations follow a strict precedence: env override (`VENICE_FORGE_CONFIG_FILE`) > repo-local (dev) > userData (packaged) > built-in defaults. The schema (v1) covers app identity, secret import policy, theme selection, default model selections, chat parameters, memory options, research defaults, character defaults, and developer flags. Plaintext `secrets.venice_api_key` / `secrets.jina_api_key` in the YAML are imported into OS secure storage (`safeStorage`) on startup and then redacted from the file (unless `secrets.keep_plaintext_keys: true` is explicitly set). Default config files never contain real keys. Three CLI scripts are bundled: `npm run config:init` (copy example templates to `.config/*.local.yaml`), `npm run config:validate` (parse + validate without launching Electron), and `npm run config:print` (print the sanitized effective config; never raw keys). A new **Settings → Local Config** section shows the resolved paths, source, parse errors, validation warnings, key import status, and provides Reload / Open Folder / Export Template / Clear Secure Store actions. See [`docs/CONFIG.md`](../DEVELOPMENT/CONFIG.md) for the full schema and security model. The local-files-only rule is enforced (`looksLikeUrl()` rejects `http://`, `https://`, and any scheme-bearing path), control characters in paths are rejected, and the existing child-safety guard runs on every prompt path regardless of config source.

### crypto primitives
./PRIVACY.md:32:- **IndexedDB:** Stores for settings, media metadata, scenes, and workflows are encrypted using AES-GCM.
./PRIVACY.md:33:- **Conversation Vault:** Current desktop conversation records are stored under `conversations/` as AES-256-GCM encrypted files.
./README.md:57:By prioritizing local data ownership, Venice Forge runs all storage operations locally on your machine—utilizing IndexedDB with AES-GCM encryption in the browser/renderer and secure OS-level keychain boundaries for credentials.
./LEGAL.md:74:Venice Forge stores chats, settings, and gallery records locally in IndexedDB. These records are encrypted by the app before storage using a browser-managed AES-GCM key stored in same-origin IndexedDB. This reduces casual local inspection risk but is not equivalent to OS credential storage. API requests still leave the device and are processed by Venice and any applicable upstream provider or privacy mode selected by Venice.

./SECURITY.md:236:- **Verifier:** `setProfilePassword(password, profileId)` stores a structured verifier record: `{ version: 1, algorithm: "pbkdf2-sha256", iterations: 310000, salt, digest }`. The salt is random per profile-password write, the digest is PBKDF2-SHA256, and verification uses `crypto.timingSafeEqual`.
